 Yes
 es
 In the production process of Menion, the course designed to separate waste materials during emissions has been recorded in the Guinness Book
 pichley saal coimbatore main unhone kachra nistaaran ke liye taiyaar apni shikshan saamagree prastut kii thi
 12,994 people participated in this for one hour
 ginis book main menian ke is shikshan kaarykram ko ricycling ke liye taiyaar ab tak ke sabase bade shikshan saamagree ke taur par darj kiya gaya he
 Menion has been working continuously for the last 15 years for environmental protection
 unke paryaavaran ke prati samarpan ko dekh kar gat varsh 5 agast ko coimbatore nagar nigam ne unhen apane shikshan paathyakram ko pesh karne kaa nyotaa diya tha
 In fact, the main objective of this learning session was to convey practical messages related to residue segregation, waste disposal, waste reuse and manure to a large number of local households
 khaas baat yah he ki paryaavarnavid na keval logon ko hi yah sikh dete hai, balki reliance industries ke pratishthanon, coloniyon or unke aas-paas ke ilaakon main bhi apana abhiyaan jor shor se chalaa rahe hai
 They have adopted several methods towards environmental protection, including storing used plastic bottles and destroying them without harming the environment
 manian kehete hai, "ye pariyojnaayen mere liye kaaphi mahatvapurn hai
 It is not that i have done all this to register my name in the Guinness Book, but for the betterment of society
 " Menion is also associated with a number of non-governmental organizations (ngos) that are involved in the restoration of water sources and plantations
 aisa hi ek sanghathan 'named siruthuli' he jo jal sroton ke navinikaran, vriksharopan, kachra prabandhan ke saath-saath jaagrukta abhiyaan chalaata he
 The comments manian ke abhiyaan par reliance industries ke pravaktaa ne kaha, "yah apshisht ke punaravartan, pun: upyog or use kam karne ke prati hamaari company kii patibaddhta ko darshata he
 Our company reuses plastics to stop using cancer-causing asbestos
 iske alaava hanikaarak rangon se nijaat paane hetu rangeen fabric kaa istemaal karti he
 It is truly an inspiration for Swachh Bharat Abhiyan
 " He said that his strategy is to safely dispose of plastic bottles, create a systematic system for their storage and fabricate them
 unhone kaha ki bade-bade aayojanon jaise ipel maichon aadi main kachra nistaaran se sambandhit hordigs lagaakar jaagrukta bhi failaate hai
 The Guinness Book records this mainline education program as the largest teaching material ever designed for recycling
 manian pichley 15 varsho se lagaataar paryaavaran sangrakshan ke liye kaam kar rahe hai
 Seeing his devotion to the environment, on 5 August last year, the Coimbatore Municipal Corporation invited him to present his teaching course
 darasal is shikshan satr kaa kaa mukhya makasad avshesh pruthakkaran, kachare kaa nistaaran, kachare ko phir se upyog ke liye taiyaar karnaa or usase khaad banane se sambandhit vyaavhaarik sandesh badi sankhya main sthaneey gharon tak pahunchaana tha
